# <a name="msmq-configuration-class"></a><span data-ttu-id="968cf-106">MSMQ-Configuration 類別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="968cf-106">MSMQ-Configuration class</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="968cf-107">此物件包含特定電腦的 MSMQ 設定參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="968cf-107">This object contains MSMQ configuration parameters for a specific computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="968cf-108">此類別的屬性是 MSMQ 特定的，而且會用於 MSMQ 路由決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="968cf-108">The attributes of this class are MSMQ specific, and are used for MSMQ routing decisions.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="968cf-117">更新頻率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="968cf-117">Update Frequency</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="968cf-118">每一部安裝 MSMQ 之電腦的電腦物件下，都會建立這個類別的實例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="968cf-118">An instance of this class is created per each computer that installs MSMQ, under the computer object.</span></span> |
